National Goods Maintenance Association Requests Postponement of Income Tax Collection; Re-implement According to Regulations Once People's Strength is Somewhat Sufficient

The China National Goods Maintenance Association sent a telegram to the National Government's Executive Yuan and Ministry of Finance requesting the postponement of income tax collection, which reads: "To Chairman Lin of the Nanjing National Government, Premier Jiang of the Executive Yuan, and Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance: We have recently read in the newspapers that the 'Provisional Regulations on Central Collection of Income Tax' are awaiting revision and implementation. According to the draft, the principles for tax collection are divided into three major categories. Except for the income of government agencies, public officials, and educational charities, all others must be collected progressively according to the amount, which is very detailed. Income tax is indeed a direct and good tax, but applying it to the current situation of widespread economic depression in our country, depleted rural economies, and declining industrial and commercial businesses is no different from giving a strong medicine to a critically ill person. The state's tax revenue may not be slightly increased, but the people's livelihoods are already on the verge of collapse. It does not seem that our government, in starting anew with the people and striving for good governance, can bear to do this. For the sake of maintaining the people's livelihood and recuperating the people's strength, our association sends this special telegram to respectfully state our case. We earnestly request your Excellency the Executive Yuan and the Ministry to be mindful of the people's difficulties and to approve a temporary postponement of income tax collection. Re-implement according to regulations once the people's strength is somewhat sufficient. We are waiting anxiously for your decision. Respectfully, Wang Jiean, Zai Xingyi, and Wang Hanqiang, Standing Committee Members of the China National Goods Maintenance Association."

Case of Recovering Extraterritorial Telephone Rights; Agreement to Jointly Establish a Business Organization; Capital Still Under Negotiation, Modeled After Water and Electricity Management; Temporary Contract to be Signed Next Month Will Be Revised

Regarding the issue of recovering telephone rights in the extraterritorial road area of Shanghai, after the Ministry of Communications dispatched personnel to Shanghai to negotiate, a compromise solution has been decided. An independent organization will be jointly established, modeled after the extraterritorial water and electricity management. The required capital is still being estimated and negotiated, and various parties will jointly subscribe for it. It is expected to be implemented within this year. The Dagong News Agency reporter has learned the details as follows:

Negotiation Process by Personnel Dispatched by the Ministry of Communications

Regarding the issue of recovering and independently operating telephones in the extraterritorial road sections of the concession area, the Ministry of Communications dispatched Section Chief Huang of the Directorate General of Telegraphs to Shanghai at the beginning of this month to exchange opinions with various parties involved. After negotiations with the authorities of the concession telephone company, a compromise solution has been reached. The company also expressed its approval of the principle of recovering sovereignty and business cooperation. Section Chief Huang has now returned to Beijing to report to the Ministry of Communications.

The Amount of Capital to be Jointly Raised Still Needs to be Negotiated

After the extraterritorial telephone rights are recovered by China, the business portion will still be operated through cooperation. A separate telephone company will be established in the extraterritorial area, modeled after the water and electricity supply method. The amount of capital is still under negotiation and will be jointly raised by the Ministry of Communications, the Shanghai Municipal Government, the concession's Public Works Department, and the Shanghai Telephone Company. It is said that China will hold 60% of the shares, and the concession will hold 40%. This method seems to be a joint business venture in form, but it is actually a preliminary measure to ease the situation. It has already achieved considerable success in recovering telephone sovereignty.

Temporary Meeting to Revise

The draft agreement for the recovery of telephone rights has been agreed upon by both parties and must be reviewed by the highest authorities before being issued to the competent authorities for handling. It is reported that the signing ceremony will be held in August or September, and the joint establishment of the telephone organization may be realized within this year. As for the temporary agreement signed in the past between the concession and the Chinese area, it will be revised after the official agreement to recover the telephone rights is signed and implemented.

Collapsing Rickshaw Mutual Aid Society Writes to the Public Works Department Requesting a Flexible Licensing Method

The Collapsing Rickshaw Industry Mutual Aid Society of this city sent a letter to the Public Works Department yesterday, requesting a flexible licensing method, which reads: "To Whom It May Concern: It has always been the practice to present a police donation ticket when donating and applying for licenses for collapsing rickshaws and tiger rickshaws. However, according to the facts, collapsing rickshaws and tiger rickshaws are all laborers who work hard for a living, and very few can hold this donation ticket. Therefore, when they donate and apply for licenses, they all borrow from others. This is because these laborers have no fixed place of residence on weekdays, which makes it difficult to inquire about them when something happens. The guarantee that your department investigates as a guarantee for issuing licenses has also lost its effectiveness. Regarding this matter, our association sent a letter to your department on June 20th, stating our case and suggesting that in the future, the donation certificates for collapsing rickshaws and tiger rickshaws should be changed to be certified by our association, and we will supervise the license holders to ensure that they abide by the general regulations related to traffic and transportation, in order to reduce your department's concerns. We subsequently received a reply on July 9th, stating that the suggested method was difficult to approve. According to our association, this suggestion not only reduces the labor of the laborers but also helps your department's vehicle management. Therefore, we reiterate our previous request and earnestly beg you to consider the difficulty of laborers donating and applying for licenses with tickets, and to make a decision and implement it. We also hope to receive a reply."

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Tenders for Stevedore Services

Ministry Orders Promulgate Bidding Rules

Since the reorganization of the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, all branches and ships have been successively restructured and ready, and business development and travel convenience have been praised, with remarkable results. The business of the warehouses and docks is more complicated, so the Ministry ordered the establishment of a Warehouse Management Office to specialize in this matter. The warehouse restructuring method has been drafted and implemented, and the stevedore services will also be tendered for contractors. All bidding rules have been promulgated by the Ministry Order. As for the bidding date, the company will publish a notice in the newspaper in the next few days. The rules are as follows: Rules of the State-Owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company for Tendering and Contracting Stevedore Services in Shanghai Warehouses: Article 1: Anyone with experience and ability to handle cargo stevedore services (loading and unloading cargo) may bid to contract the cargo stevedore services of the company's Shanghai warehouses in accordance with these rules. Article 2: The warehouses for which the company is tendering stevedore services are as follows: (A) China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's South Warehouse at No. 16 Pu, Shanghai (i.e., Jinliyuan Wharf); (B) China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's North Warehouse on East Broadway Road, Shanghai; (C) China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Central Warehouse on Avenue Joffre, Shanghai; (D) China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's New Warehouse in Yangjiadu, Pudong; (E) China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's China Warehouse in 18 Jian, Pudong. Article 3: Bidders must first pay a bidding deposit of 500 yuan in national currency (cash or bank draft) to the company, and the company will issue a receipt as proof, and receive the printed bid form, bid envelope, resume form, and draft contract. Article 4: Bidders should fill in each item on the company's bid form in detail and clearly, sign and seal it, and place it together with the draft contract in the bid envelope, seal it tightly with sealing wax, seal it with a seal, and personally put it into the bid box on the day of voting. Bids that do not use the company's bid form or bid envelope, or are not filled in according to the format, or are altered, will be invalidated. Article 5: The bidding for each warehouse listed in Article 2 will be held separately in sequence. Bidders may not bid for other warehouses when bidding for each warehouse. A winning bidder for any warehouse may not be a bidder for any other warehouse. Article 6: After the public opening of bids, the company will select one winning bidder and one alternate winning bidder for each warehouse from the bids submitted, based on the lowest price and abundant experience, and notify them in writing. If the company believes that none of the bid prices submitted by the bidders are qualified, it may reschedule the bidding. Article 7: The winning bidder shall, within five days after the company issues a written notice, invite a shareholder and a substantial shop to come to the company to sign a contract (the formal contract will be handled in accordance with the draft contract attached to the bid receipt, and the bidder shall not request modification), and return the bidding deposit based on the certificate, and separately pay the contracting stevedore deposit, and the company will issue a receipt for storage. The amount of deposit for each warehouse is stipulated as follows: (A) South Warehouse stevedore cash guarantee of 15,000 yuan in national currency, substantial shop guarantee of 20,000 yuan; (B) North Warehouse stevedore cash guarantee of 10,000 yuan in national currency, substantial shop guarantee of 10,000 yuan; (C) Central Warehouse stevedore cash guarantee of 10,000 yuan in national currency, substantial shop guarantee of 10,000 yuan; (D) New Warehouse stevedore cash guarantee of 5,000 yuan in national currency, substantial shop guarantee of 5,000 yuan; (E) China Warehouse stevedore cash guarantee of 5,000 yuan in national currency, substantial shop guarantee of 5,000 yuan. Article 8: If the winning bidder fails to come to the company to sign the contract within the time limit set by the company, the company will confiscate the 500 yuan bidding deposit and may successively replace it with the alternate winning bidder. Article 9: The winning bidder shall, within 15 days from the date of signing the contract, appoint all hired employees and start taking over the stevedore services. If it cannot be implemented after the deadline, all the cash stevedore deposit paid will be confiscated, and it will be successively replaced by the alternate winning bidder. Article 10: The bidding deposit of the unsuccessful bidder will be notified to come to the company within three days after the company decides on the winning bidder, and will be returned upon receipt. However, the bidding deposit of the alternate winning bidder shall be returned upon receipt of the company's notice after the winning bidder starts to undertake the stevedore services. After signing the contract, the winning bidder's bidding deposit shall be used to offset part of the cash stevedore deposit based on the certificate. Article 11: Before receiving the notice to collect the bidding deposit, the alternate winning bidder has the obligation to be called to sign the contract at any time. If the contract cannot be signed as scheduled after notification, the company may confiscate the bidding deposit paid by the alternate winning bidder. Note: This rule is accompanied by a percentage table of the main goods in each warehouse for reference by bidders.

Opening of the Chinese Cultural Relics Exhibition

The Chinese Cultural Relics Exhibition at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Seymour Road was officially opened by Mayor Wu at 10:00 AM yesterday. Many Chinese and Western guests attended, and more than 2,000 people visited throughout the day. The items displayed inside the venue are all top-quality treasures, many of which have never been seen by people in Shanghai. They are comparable to the exhibits that participated in the London International Art Exhibition last year. The exhibits are divided into two parts: one part is non-sale items, which are all rare and unique copies collected by private individuals, and the value is not marked; the other part is for sale items, which are all documented and can be confirmed. A large number were sold yesterday, especially books, paintings, ceramics, copper, and carvings. It is said that the exhibition will close on the 31st of this month, lasting only ten days.

The Executive Yuan Orders a Ban on Yellow River and Charity Lottery Tickets

The Yellow River Flood Relief Lottery issued by Hebei Province previously had a limit of twelve issues and ended as scheduled. In April of this year, the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee requested to continue issuing the Yellow River Flood Relief Lottery to raise funds for relief, as the Yellow River's aftermath in Hebei had not been resolved. The Ministry of Finance replied that the lottery was issued temporarily as a matter of expediency for urgent relief, and it seemed inappropriate to continue issuing it. Moreover, the plan for both addressing the symptoms and root causes of the Yellow River flood had already been handled by the responsible agency, so there seemed to be no need to continue issuing the lottery. The Executive Yuan had already ordered the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee to comply. However, in the past two months, the Yellow River Flood Relief Lottery has continued to be issued, and the Tianjin Municipal Public Welfare Charity Lottery has also been promoted in various places. It has been found that neither of these lotteries has been approved by the government and should be strictly prohibited from sale to maintain the law. The Executive Yuan approved the Ministry of Finance's reply, stating that since there was no need to continue issuing the Yellow River lottery, and the so-called Tianjin Municipal Public Welfare Charity Lottery had not been reported, it should be strictly prohibited. A special telegram was sent to the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee, ordering it to investigate and terminate the issuance and instructed the provincial and municipal governments to comply and instruct their subordinates to strictly prohibit sales.

The Maid of Xie Xifan's Family Threw Away a Cannonball

Picked Up During the Zhili-Fengtian War; Sent to the Public Security Bureau for Storage

A certain maid of the Yong-native Xie Xifan's family, who lives at No. 29 Fangxie Road in Nanshi, discarded a cannonball in a nearby trash can at around 9:00 AM yesterday. It was noticed by a cleaner who retrieved the cannonball and sent it to the Ximen Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for verification. Director Yao of the branch sent police to summon Xie Xifan to the bureau for questioning. According to Xie's confession, the cannonball was brought back from the countryside during the Zhili-Fengtian War in the autumn of 1925 and kept as a war souvenir. Now, it was found by someone in the family during cleaning and discarded into the trash can by the maid. He requested identification, etc. Xie was ordered to hand over the confiscated cannonball and send it to the General Bureau for storage.

Another Rickshaw Theft Occurs in the French Concession

Since the French Concession authorities arrested and severely punished the main culprits involved in rickshaw thefts last December, there had been no reported cases of stolen rickshaws for several months. However, Jin Senchang, a rickshaw puller residing at 207 Shangwen Road, working for the Li Ji Rickshaw Company, and pulling rickshaw with city permit number 4357 and French permit number 11886, lost his rickshaw at 1 AM on the 18th of this month. He had left the rickshaw briefly to pick up a customer south of the Huangjin Grand Theatre on Eight Immortals Bridge, and in a blink of an eye, the rickshaw disappeared. He immediately reported the theft to nearby patrol officers and detectives, and also reported the theft to the Songshan Road Police Station, requesting that they investigate and recover the rickshaw and apprehend the thief. The Rickshaw Guild also reported the situation to the French Concession Police Department to prevent a resurgence of such crimes, which would affect the livelihoods of the poor. It is reported that the rickshaw puller has been searching the streets daily since the theft, as he has no rickshaw to pull, and his situation is quite miserable.

Silk and Satin Guild Announces Price Increase for Suzhou Goods

Raw Silk Prices Soar, Increasing Costs by One to Two and a Half 分 Per 钱

The Shanghai Silk and Satin Trade Association issued a notice regarding the price increase of newly woven Suzhou silk and satin: "This year's new silk has entered the market with extraordinarily high prices, and raw silk has soared in particular. To ensure cost recovery, we must appropriately increase the prices of goods. The association has resolved that, effective immediately, iron loom goods such as patterned crepe will temporarily increase by one 分 per 钱 compared to spring prices, while wooden loom goods such as figured and plain satin will temporarily increase by two and a half 分 per 钱 to maintain the current situation. In addition to notifying all member stores to comply, we are issuing this public notice. As the silk price increase trend has not yet stopped, whether or not to continue to increase prices will be discussed again depending on market conditions."

Worker Dies in Nanjing Theatre Repair in Nanjing

Fang Shunxiao, a Yongbo native, aged 38, a painter residing at the Yongxing Road entrance of the Gonghe Xin Road in Zhabei, was dispatched by the Shen Rongji Paint Shop at No. 18 Xiaotaoyuan Lane on Rue Lafayette in the French Concession to do painting work at the Nanjing Theatre on Avenue Edward VII on the 18th. At 1:15 PM that afternoon, Fang was working at a second-floor window on the east side of the theater facing Rue de la Macao, when he suddenly lost his footing and fell, injuring his head and bleeding from both ears. He immediately lost consciousness. The theatre reported the incident to the Avenue Joffre Police Station, who transported Fang to Guangci Hospital. Due to the severity of his injuries, he died shortly after arriving at the hospital. The police transported the body to the Tongren Fuyuan branch for examination. Fang Xu, his concubine, was summoned to the station. Yesterday, Prosecutor Wang Ren of the Second Special District Court, along with a forensic doctor and clerk, arrived at the station and confirmed that the deceased had died from injuries sustained in the fall. Witness Wu Ashuang (who worked with the deceased) was questioned about the incident. The court released the body to Fang Xu for burial.

Bookbinders Demand World Book Company Restore Original Prices

Workers Plan to Form "Kneeling and Crying" Group

According to Guomin She, the bookbinders who contract with the World Book Company in this city include 21 firms such as Liu Peiji, Zhou Shunji, Wang Jinji, and Sun Yongji. It is said that previously only five firms contracted with the book company, but the World Book Company has continuously added workshops, and now there are as many as 21. Every time a new binding firm is added, the binding fee is reduced once. In 1932, it was 9 角 2 分 5 厘 per ten thousand pages, and has gradually decreased to less than 6 角 per ten thousand pages now. The various bookbinders have been repeatedly reduced the binding fee by the book company, and are all feeling straitened and struggling to maintain. Now affected by the economic depression and the rising cost of living, all bookbinders feel difficult and are unable to maintain the status quo. It is learned that 21 bookbinding firms and workers are unanimously uniting to demand that the World Book Company restore original prices. It is also heard that the first step is to send representatives from the bookbinding firms to demand this from the book company. If there is no result, the workers will continue to rise up in assistance, and it is learned that the workers are planning to organize a kneeling and crying group, compile a booklet to expose the inside story of the book company, and kneel and cry to various public groups for assistance in upholding justice. The 21 bookbinding firms have sent Zhou Shunquan, Liu Peisheng, and others to the factory once to negotiate, but the company has not yet given a substantial reply.

Police Shoot Fleeing Thief; Body Recovered Yesterday

Li Suiming, a road policeman at the Wusong Machinery Factory, took the thief Xie Xiaoanzi to the Baotai Wan ship to retrieve a pawn ticket for stolen goods. When Xie was unprepared, he suddenly jumped into the river and tried to escape. Officer Li fired his gun, and Xie was hit and killed, his body sinking to the bottom of the river. Yesterday afternoon, the police hired workers to recover the body, and ordered the local head to report to the local court, which sent a prosecutor to the scene to confirm that the death was caused by a gunshot wound (the bullet entered from the back and exited from the front of the chest). The body was placed in a coffin by a charity and prepared for burial, pending investigation.

Conferring Honorary Title on Yuan's Mother Will Be Held Soon

Yuan Ludeng, a native of Ningbo, is a well-known merchant in Shanghai. His mother, Madam Hu, passed away on June 9th of this year. Because Madam Hu had a strong belief in religion during her lifetime, customs such as mourning were all eliminated. Now, those who had a past with the Yuan family believe that Madam Hu did good deeds and promoted education, and made contributions to society, so her passing cannot be without commemoration. Therefore, following the example of Song Xuanwen and Meng Deyao in ancient times, they will initiate a preparatory committee for conferring an honorary title on Yuan's mother, and circulate letters to Yuan's relatives and friends to discuss the honorary title, to highlight her virtuous qualities. Now, after more than a thousand people used written nominations, the deadline was the 15th of this month. The words "慈惠" (Cihui - Benevolent and Kind) were the most numerous, so she is called Madam Cihui, and they plan to choose a day to hold the ceremony of conferring the honorary title, to show solemnity. It is heard that recently those who have joined the ceremony are still continuously increasing, and the ceremony will definitely be a lively affair in the future.

Page 14

Inmates Riot and Escape; Responsible Persons Must Be Severely Punished According to Law; Escaped Inmates Must Be Apprehended Within a Limited Time; Heads of Respective Institutions Should Also Be Disciplined

The Special District Court of Shanghai received an instruction from the Ministry of Judicial Administration yesterday: "Recently, cases of inmates in prisons escaping have been occurring almost daily in various provinces, and cases of inmates rioting in groups are also frequently seen. Although this is due to the imperfect construction of prisons in various counties, it is also due to the lack of effective supervision by prison officials. However, a major reason is the failure to provide thorough warnings regarding the various laws concerning the escape of inmates beforehand, and the failure to strictly enforce them afterwards. All prisons should be ordered to promptly compile matters for inmates to comply with while in prison, and to appropriately add and revise the matters for inmates to comply with while in prison promulgated by the Beijing Ministry of Justice two years ago, and to include the full text of Article 161 and Article 162 of the Criminal Law, Article 1, Paragraph 19 of the Provisional Measures for Handling Banditry Cases promulgated by the Central Government in August of last year, and Article 29 of the Inmate Regulations and Article 43 of the Detention Center Regulations, and print multiple copies for posting in the wards for reading. Those who are illiterate should be explained in detail to provide a warning. The responsibilities of prison staff and their supervisors have already been stipulated and notified in Article 161 of the Criminal Law and this Ministry's Instruction No. 5562 last year, respectively, and are hereby notified again for compliance. Hereafter, attention must be paid to organizing matters for reducing inmates' protection in various prisons. If there are any more escapes, the escaped inmates will certainly be apprehended within a limited time and severely punished according to law. If the personnel responsible for the prison are involved in criminal suspicion, they should also be severely punished according to law, and the heads of the respective institutions should also be disciplined in accordance with the previous order, and no leniency will be shown. Each must obey respectfully and not neglect."

Female Thief Sentenced

Chen Meizhen, a Suzhou woman residing at Tai'an Lane, 207 Rue Bayle, French Concession, was broken into at night in March of this year by her fellow townsman Ma Laoliu, who used to work with her in a room at the Changsan brothel, and two men. They displayed a handgun, first blindfolded Chen Meizhen, and then, directed by Ma Laoliu, searched and stole a diamond ring, gold jewelry, and cash, totaling over 700 yuan. They then fled. During the robbery, the blindfold on Meizhen's face loosened, allowing her to recognize the female thief's face and report it to the police. The suspect was not apprehended until the end of last month, when the victim encountered Ma Laoliu near the intersection of Zhejiang Road and Avenue du Contre Amiral Courbet in the Public Concession. She stepped forward and apprehended her, and called the police to take her to the police station, which transferred her to the French Concession Police Station. According to Ma's confession, she went to commit the robbery with her estranged lover Pan Haiyuan and Pan's younger brother A Si, who is still at large. Pan Haiyuan was arrested and sent to the Second Special District Court for investigation and detention. Investigator Liu Jinrong checked with the silver shop and found the date when Ma Laoliu sold the jewelry, and a receipt was reissued and sent to the court. The Police Department filed a public prosecution for robbery. During the trial presided over by Judge Li Changnian, Ma Laoliu claimed that she had borrowed money from the plaintiff unsuccessfully and took the opportunity to commit a theft, denying that she had organized a robbery. Pan Haiyuan denied any involvement and claimed to have been falsely accused, and each hired a lawyer to defend them. The details had been reported in this newspaper. The case has now concluded. At 8 AM the day before yesterday, Judge Li delivered his verdict in Criminal Division One, sentencing Ma Laoliu to six months in prison and acquitting Pan Haiyuan. During the appeal period, Ma will be held in detention, and Pan is allowed bail pending a decision.

Liu Haisu Exhibition Closed Yesterday

Russian Ambassador and Sun Yat-sen Institute President Visited the Exhibition; Liu Haisu's art exhibition closed yesterday, the last day, at 1 PM. Visitors continued to arrive in an endless stream. Russian Ambassador Bogomolov, accompanied by the embassy counselor and the director of the Cultural Promotion Department, as well as British Consul General Bayly, visited the exhibition for a long time and purchased the fifth painting, "Clear Pond at Noon," worth 400 yuan. The Russian ambassador highly praised Liu's art and was eager to meet him. The clerk, Song Banggan, telephoned Liu, who had just returned to Shanghai from Beijing that morning. Liu and his wife immediately went to the exhibition to greet the ambassador, and they had a very pleasant conversation. The Russian ambassador hoped that Liu could hold an exhibition in Moscow next spring, and Liu promised to consider it. Sun Ke, the President of the Legislative Yuan, Legislative Member Wu Jingxiong, Li Zhaohuan, the President of Jiaotong University, and others also visited the exhibition. They all agreed that Liu's oil paintings and traditional Chinese paintings were profound, vigorous, and creative, representing a turning point in the history of Chinese art. President Sun purchased painting number 74, "Knowing the White, Keeping the Black," and Wu Jingxiong also booked "Su Dongpo and His Two Friends."

"Women's Army" Gang Commits Violence; Bounced Check Causes Trouble

Yang Xintian, a 35-year-old Chongming native, who makes a living playing mahjong, residing at No. 5, Alley 16, Dengyun Lane, purchased 171 yuan worth of artificial mahjong tiles from Wang Bomei (30 years old), a Yongbo native, at the Xie Feng Industrial Cooperative at No. 2 Yuqing Lane, Xietu Road, last month. He signed a check from the Jianye Bank for 122 yuan, with the remaining amount to be paid at the end of the month. When Wang tried to cash the check, it bounced. Wang contacted Yang, but Yang avoided him. A few days ago, Wang happened to meet Yang Xintian at the Yiyuan Teahouse in the Chenghuangmiao Yuyuan, but Yang evaded responsibility. Wang called police officer Su Yushu to take Yang to the Chenghuangmiao Police Station for questioning. Officer Chen interrogated him and found that the case involved the use of a bounced check, which constituted fraud, and ordered that he be handed over for further investigation. Unexpectedly, at 3 PM yesterday, Yang's wife, Ms. Lu, together with her mother, Ms. Lu Shi, led several members of a "women's army" to Wang's residence, claiming that her whole family relied on her husband alone to earn a living, and that if Wang did not drop the case, her entire family would move in to live with him. Wang was out at the time. Yang and Ms. Lu returned to the Yiyuan in Chenghuangmiao to meet Wang's younger brother, Boxun, and falsely accused Boxun of using violent means to take away 42 sets of mahjong tiles worth over 200 yuan, demanding that they be used to offset the debt and that the difference be paid in cash. Boxun argued that the accusation was fabricated. During the dispute, Yang and Ms. Lu directed the "women's army" to beat Boxun over the head, and he cried out for help. When the patrol officer arrived, he only arrested the leaders Yang and Ms. Lu Shi. The injured Wang Boxun was sent to the hospital for treatment. After questioning, Officer Chen found that the defendants had committed violence with a gang, and the case involved injury, and they were handed over to the bureau for legal action.

Underage Girl Cannot File a Lawsuit Independently; Marriage Fraud and Abandonment Case Needs Review

Zhu Liangqing, the owner of the Tongtaihe cigarette paper shop at No. 193, Lane at the intersection of Old Barricade Road and Haineng Road, was recently criminally prosecuted by Ma Shanbao, a 19-year-old Suzhou woman, who hired lawyer Huang Renchong to file a case with the First Special Court for marriage fraud and abandonment. The reasons given were that Ma's father died when she was six years old, her mother died when she was twelve years old, and she relied on her maternal grandmother, Shen Xu, to raise her. In May of the year before last, her maternal grandmother was deceived by the defendant and promised Ma to the defendant for cohabitation. At that time, the plaintiff was under the age of sixteen, young and ignorant. On June 23 of that year, she began cohabiting with the defendant in the building above the bamboo shop on Peng Road, and repeatedly urged him to formally marry, but he made all sorts of excuses. In November of last year, his legal wife arrived in Shanghai, and he drove the plaintiff away, revealing that she had been deceived. The defendant's actions constitute a violation of Article 229 of the Criminal Law, using fraud to make a woman mistakenly believe that he is her spouse and submit to his adultery, and Article 294 of the same law, abandonment. The lawsuit includes civil claims and asks the court to order the payment of 15 yuan per month in living expenses from June 24 of this year until she is 60 years old. Yesterday morning, Judge Tan Xinzhen presided over the hearing in Criminal Division Eight. The defendant also hired a lawyer to defend him. After questioning, Judge Tan stated that the plaintiff, Ma Shanbao, is only 19 years old and has not yet reached adulthood, and therefore is not allowed to file a lawsuit independently according to law. Therefore, there appears to be a procedural impropriety, and the case will be reviewed and re-examined.

Zhao Heming's Concubine Flees; Ling Peng Accused of Enticement; Cohabitant Introduced Them; Once Planned to Escape to Ningbo

Zhao Heming, a local resident residing at 57 Pingliang Road, 26 years old, recently hired lawyers Li Lin and Xi Xiaoruo to file a criminal complaint with the First Special Court against Ling Peng and Song Peigen for attempting to entice a woman under the age of 20 away from her family, and filed a civil lawsuit along with it. The statement of claim stated that the plaintiff's concubine, Ying Xiuzhen, 19 years old, had been cohabiting with the plaintiff at No. 7, Lane 57, Pingliang Road. On June 9 of this year, Ying Xiuzhen suddenly ran away while the plaintiff was out. Before leaving, she left a note falsely claiming that she was returning to her mother's home in Ningbo. The plaintiff initially did not suspect anything. On the 15th of the same month, he discovered that 800 yuan in cash and jewelry and clothing that he had purchased for Ying Xiuzhen, which he had hidden in an iron box, had disappeared. He suspected that she had run away and sent a telegram to Ningbo to inquire at Ying's mother's house. They replied that she had not returned to Ningbo. He then investigated everywhere, and on the 23rd, he found Ying Xiuzhen hiding at Yan Shanmei's place, a "little sister," at No. 34 Lishi Lane, Lujiabang, Nanshi. He reported the incident to the police, who arrested Ying and Yan and sent them to the Shanghai Local Court. According to Ying Xiuzhen's confession, her departure was due to Song Peigen, who lived in the same house as the plaintiff, acting as an intermediary. She met Ling Peng and became intimate with him. Ling had originally planned to take her to Ningbo on June 8. However, because she felt it was inappropriate, she did not go. Ling missed his stop and was taken to Ningbo. The next day, he called her, asking her to take the cash and go to Ningbo. Ling waited at the dock and invited her to the Dongya Hotel in Ningbo, and then they returned to Shanghai, renting a house at No. 375 Penglai Road. The 800 yuan in cash that she had taken was taken out and used by Ling. Therefore, the defendants have clearly violated Article 240, Paragraphs 1 and 3 of the Criminal Law, and the lawsuit includes civil claims, asking the court to order compensation of 800 yuan in national currency. Yesterday morning, Presiding Judge Qian Hongye presided over the hearing in the Criminal Court. Neither of the defendants arrived, and each commissioned a lawyer to appear in court and request a postponement. The plaintiff, Zhao Heming, submitted the case, stating the above situation. The court decided that because the defendants had not arrived, the hearing would be rescheduled in seven days.

China Poultry Association Presents to Ministry of Education: Unify Translated Names of Poultry Books

In recent years, the new method of poultry farming in our country has become increasingly popular thanks to the efforts and promotion of various poultry farming academic organizations. There are also many books on poultry farming published in the market. However, most of the books are translated from Europe, America, and Japan. Due to differences in translation styles, the translated academic and breed names are also different. The same English name, after being translated into Chinese, has as many as four or five different versions. This creates many obstacles to academic research and promotion. The China Poultry Academic Research Association at No. 534 Xiangyin Road in the city center submitted a request to the Ministry of Education yesterday, asking to unify the translated names of poultry farming academics and breeds nationwide. At the same time, the president of the association, Zhang Ruizhi, has prepared a complete list of translated names for the Ministry of Education's reference.

Abduction Case Awaiting Sentencing

Xiao Mei, the seven-year-old daughter of Xu Liyuan, a Ningbo native residing at No. 57 Xinwen Road, disappeared while playing at the back door at 5 PM on the 8th of this month. He asked people to search for her without success and reported the situation to the Hongkou Police Station. After investigation by Chinese Detective Zhang Faxiang, it was learned that Wu Aisheng, a Wuxi native residing at No. 33 Rue d'Euclidis had a relationship with the case. He was arrested and confessed that Xu's daughter was hidden at No. 57 Shajing Road by a person named Xiao Chen. They rushed to the address to arrest them. Xiao Chen escaped upon hearing the news. Xu's daughter was found downstairs and brought to the police station. The next morning, the suspect was sent to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention. The girl was returned to her father. During the rescheduling, Detective Zhang learned that there was an accomplice, Niu Boliang, from Songjiang, hiding at No. 274 Menggu Road, Zhabei. He secretly contacted the public security bureau of the jurisdiction and arrested Niu at the address. He was brought back to the police station. Yesterday, he and Wu were sent to Criminal Division Three. Lawyer Zhang Shizhu of the Public Works Department stated that it was found that the two defendants, together with Xiao Chen who was at large, had abducted two girls, one four years old and one eight years old, from a certain place between December of last year and February of this year. They were sold to Chen Peichang at No. 16 Rue d'Euclidis, the eight-year-old girl for 40 yuan and the four-year-old girl for 26 yuan, and the money was divided and spent. Currently, Chen Peichang at No. 16 Rue d'Euclidis has fled without a trace due to unpaid rent, and he cannot be arrested. The families of the two girls cannot be found and identified. It is requested that the case be punished according to law. Judge Xiao Fenfen questioned the two defendants clearly and ordered them to be detained pending sentencing.

House Collapse Injures People in West Shanghai

The three side rooms of the house of Jiang Yuqin, a local who works at the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Transfer Company, collapsed at No. 24 Jiangjiatang in the south of Hongqiao Town in West Shanghai. Due to years of disrepair, the beams and pillars were decaying, and coupled with the continuous strong winds and heavy rains, the entire hall collapsed suddenly at about 5 PM yesterday, causing a loss of about 200 yuan. Yuqin's wife, Ms. Gu, was at home in Shanghai at the time. Only his elderly mother, Ms. Wang, was unable to escape in time and was severely injured. She is now being sent to the hospital for treatment.

Shop Assistant Seduces Shop Owner's Daughter; Secret Pregnancy, They Flee Together; Tracked Down and Arrested

Bao Hefeng, a Ningbo native, runs a cigarette paper and sundry goods shop at No. 1209 Qujiang Road in Zhabei. Bao has a daughter named Aizhu, 19 years old, who is studying at junior high school. There was a shop assistant named Huang Jinbao, from Wangqiao, Xicheng Town, outside the West Gate of Jiading County. Seeing that Aizhu had some beauty, he seduced her into an affair. Recently, because Aizhu was four months pregnant and afraid of being discovered by her parents, Huang Jinbao accompanied her to Jiading on a Xihu long-distance bus on the 15th of this month. They temporarily rented a Pan-family house outside the West Gate as a place to hide her. When Aizhu left home, she left a letter stating that she was going out to commit suicide because she was not free. But Aizhu's parents already knew that she had been lured out by Huang Jinbao, so they sent their son-in-law, Xu Zhongsheng, to Jiading to find her. He found her at the Pan family's house outside the West Gate. He reported the incident to the police and arrested Aizhu, Huang Jinbao, and Huang's brother, Mu Liang. At the same time, Aizhu's mother and brother, Hu Tianyi, also heard the news and rushed to the Jiading County Public Security Bureau, asking them to transfer the case to the county government for trial.

Ship Hand Falls into River; Body Missing

Yuan Xiaohua, 24 years old, a local resident, was a ship hand in the Huangpu River. At 10 AM yesterday, he and another ship hand were carrying passengers across the river. When the boat reached the Huangpu River off Shenjiahuayuan, Yuan went to the stern to get something, walking along the side of the boat. However, there were many ships at the time, and the waves were surging. The boat shook, and Yuan lost his footing, fell into the river, and drowned. His fellow ship hand, Lu Xiaocai, saw this and stopped the boat to search for him, but the body could not be found. He submitted a report to the city's river patrol team, requesting that they find the whereabouts of the body.

County Government Maintains Waterborne Security

The Shanghai County Government hereby investigates that the jurisdiction of this county often connects to the Huangpu River, where bandit gangs can easily emerge. Recently, incidents of robbery on land and water have occurred repeatedly. Land-based defense has already been strengthened by the Public Security Bureau and security teams. However, waterborne defense should also be given attention to ensure that bandit gangs have no place to stand. In addition to following provincial orders to instruct all districts to organize waterborne Baobias, given the unpredictable nature of vessels in the Huangpu River, thoroughness cannot be expected without regular inspections. Orders have now been issued for each district to establish offices separately, assign personnel to be responsible for handling, to eradicate bandit traces and maintain security.

Sichuan Opera Troupe Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday, Performance at Xin Guang Soon

The Chengdu-Chongqing Sichuan Opera Troupe is an organization of provincial dramatic arts elites, with outstanding talent. Their performances are no less than the finest Peking Opera and Yue Opera. The Ga腔 (Gao Qiang) and Xi调 (Xi Diao) styles in the opera are particularly unique in flavor. Therefore, their recorded songs are popular not only domestically, but also sought after by European and American dramatists and musicians, which demonstrates their high value. The troupe of over a hundred people, led by Mr. Lu Han Chen and Mr. Deng Zhi Fu, came east and arrived in Shanghai yesterday. They have already leased the Xin Guang Grand Theatre and will meet with Shanghai audiences as soon as the program is arranged.

Doctor Ma Yuanlong Moves Practice

Dr. Ma Yuanlong, a famous physician from Shanghai's Yu district, specializes in internal and external medicine. Since coming to Shanghai County, it has been over ten years. His medical knowledge is profound, and he has saved countless lives, leading to a growing reputation and fame. Recently, due to busy practice, the original address was insufficient, so he has moved to No. 30 Shiyu Fang, Chengdu Road, telephone number 34010. During this hot summer, he is holding free clinics from 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM, with a registration fee of two Jiao. Therefore, those seeking treatment have been crowding the door lately. It is heard that the Modern Travel Agency in the Zhonghui Building on Avenue Edward VII has also hired Dr. Ma as a year-round medical consultant due to the large number of employees. He will be at the agency from 3:00 PM to 7:00 PM every afternoon for consultations, with a registration fee of four Jiao for Modern Travel Agency employees or those introduced by employees.

Missing Girl from Xu Residence

Our reporter, Xu Chengxu, currently resides at No. 2 Songqing Li, next to the Empire Theatre on Avenue Joffre in the French Concession. Around 10:00 AM yesterday, a girl went missing. The girl's name is Xiao Yatou, she is eleven years old, wearing white cloth shirt and pants, with a Yangzhou accent, somewhat able to speak Shanghainese, short and chubby build, thick eyebrows and large eyes, hair not tied and no socks. Anyone who sees and temporarily keeps her, please notify Mr. Xu at the address, and there will be a considerable reward.

Silk and Cotton Industry Public Association Executive Committee Meeting

The Shanghai Silk and Cotton Industry Association held an executive committee meeting yesterday, with Chairman Tang Huanquan and Recorder Jia Wenbiao. After formalities, Jiang Yongchun, Lu Huansheng, and Tang Huanquan were appointed as standing committee members, and Tang Huanquan was elected as chairman. Discussion items: Regarding how to regulate the increased prices of silk and cotton from the brokers, it was resolved to follow the resolutions of the previous representative conference. The price increase for each Jin of silk and cotton from the brokers is four Jiao, and it is stipulated that there should be no infighting among the industry. If old customers' business is received, 40% will be handed over for equal distribution. Regarding the date of commencement of monthly fees, it was resolved to collect from July onwards, with silk and cotton shops paying two Yuan per month, and brokers extracting five Fen per Jin as a subsidy for insufficient funds. (Other items omitted)

Guan Sheng Yuan Sells Small Goldfish: The Jin Yu (Goldfish) Department of Guan Sheng Yuan Farm in Caohejing is large in scale and well-organized, collecting various goldfish from the North and South, no less than forty or fifty types, managed by experts, scientifically raised. This year's fish are especially abundant, with a total number of over 200,000, which can be considered the best goldfish garden in Shanghai. Recently, specially made beautiful glass cups have been ordered, several hundred dozen, each containing several colorful small goldfish, priced at two Jiao per cup. All branches and dining departments are selling them. At this time of intense summer heat, having one or two on the desk can clear the mind and refresh the spirit. They are truly a wonderful product for cooling off in the summer.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast for 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Shandong is surrounded by cloudy and clear, hot weather, with a southeasterly wind. The upper and middle reaches of the Yellow River and the upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River have light winds with variable directions. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and the East Sea are cloudy with thunderstorms and a southeasterly wind. The typhoon in the Pacific Ocean is still moving northwest. The typhoon in Dongsha Island will move northwest. The first typhoon's center point reached within about 120 miles of 16 degrees north latitude and 116 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM. At the same time, the second typhoon's center point reached within about 60 miles of 17 degrees north latitude and 112 degrees east longitude. The wind force of both typhoons is unknown. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 89.6 and the lowest was 77.5. On the same day last year, the highest was 98.1 and the lowest was 79.5.

Letter to the Editor

To the esteemed editor, upon reading a news item titled "Theft of Large Amount of Cigarettes Solved in Nanhui County Bandit Hideout" on page 13 of section 4 of your newspaper dated July 17, which stated that the original cigarette thief was found at the residence of Baozhang Pan Xukui in our township, and Wu Jiasheng, who was arrested, confessed to the water patrol that he was the deputy head of the Xiukang Township Defense Corps in the Fifth District of Nanhui County, we were shocked. After investigation, our township has a total of thirteen Baos, and there is no such person as Pan Shukui among the thirteen Baozhangs. Moreover, the Baozhangs of each Bao were issued appointment letters by the District Office at that time and reported to the County Government. Since he is neither the former nor the current officer, how could he falsely claim the position? It is extremely despicable. Now, for the sake of credibility among all sectors, we must disclose the names of the thirteen Baozhangs in our township one by one, which are: Liu Xingen, Baozhang of the first Bao; Ding Zhiying, Baozhang of the second Bao; Ye Yizhang, Baozhang of the third Bao; Ding Miaosheng, Baozhang of the fourth Bao; Zhang Guiqing, Baozhang of the fifth Bao; Zhang Zhenlin, Baozhang of the sixth Bao; Qin Xingeng, Baozhang of the seventh Bao; Fan Chunsheng, Baozhang of the eighth Bao; Zhang Fuxiu, Baozhang of the ninth Bao; Cao Fuxi, Baozhang of the tenth Bao; Zhu Caigen, Baozhang of the eleventh Bao; Wang Julin, Baozhang of the twelfth Bao; Yao Zhanglong, Baozhang of the thirteenth Bao. Furthermore, the accomplice named Wu Jiasheng does not reside in our township and is not the deputy head of the Defense Corps of our township. This can be easily inquired and verified, and it is not difficult to clarify the truth. We suspect that the reporter at the time may have reported inaccurate rumors. We are deeply concerned that such an error will affect the reputation of our township office. We hereby request that the editor make a correction in the letter to the editor section of your newspaper. Sincerely, Wang Julin, Township Head of Xiukang Township, Fifth District, Nanhui County, July 18.

Acknowledgement: We thank the Commercial Press for donating one copy each of the Oriental Magazine, Volume 33, Issue 14, the English Weekly, Issue 190, and the Children's Newspaper, Issue 90. Thank you.

Davis Cup Trial Match United States Wins 3-2 over Great Britain Pan Lei and Boqi in Epic Unresolved Battle Grant Defeats Austin in Straight Sets

Ten Countries Participating in This Year's Olympic Football Tournament England Has Not Yet Registered But Is Prepared to Participate The Netherlands Has Difficulty Resolving the Problem of Player Salary Losses

(Berlin Correspondence) Football - the "King of Balls" - has more changes in the history of the Olympic Games than other sports. Since 1908, it has been listed as one of the Olympic events. When the Olympic Games were held in Amsterdam, the Netherlands, in 1928, opinions differed on whether the football teams had violated the Olympic amateur rules, which involved the entire football participation in the Olympic Games. The dispute was intense and difficult to resolve. In the end, the opposition won, so the football competition was cancelled when the 10th Olympic Games were held in Los Angeles, USA, in 1932. However, in the International Football Association convened in Rome in the autumn of 1934, it was decided that football would still be included in the Olympic program, so that football teams from various countries could participate in the competition. This resolution did not contradict the original intention of cancelling participation due to amateur problems, but rather to increase the interest of the Olympic Committee itself. The Olympic Games to be held in Berlin this summer will implement this resolution and add football competitions, and many have now joined.

Twenty countries have already participated in the football competition of this year's World Games, and the registration procedures have been completed long ago. However, England, which is known for football, has not yet made a move. Football is most common in England, so whether England will participate is a major issue that has attracted the attention of the world. According to the 4th and 5th World Games held in London in 1908 and Stockholm in 1912, the football championships were won by England. England did not participate in the 8th and 9th World Games held in Paris and Amsterdam. The proposal to participate in the Berlin World Games this year was put forward by Dr. Bao Wen, a international referee. He has already submitted a written proposal to prepare for participation, and at the same time, he is soliciting opinions from the best amateur teams in England. A final decision will be made soon. News from London says that England can organize a strong football team to participate in this year's World Games.

Whether the Netherlands will send a football team to participate in the World Games is also a serious issue for the Dutch sports community. It is the general opinion that the Royal Dutch Football Association should organize a team to participate, because the Netherlands is a first-class football country, so the Netherlands not sending a football team is the same as the United States not sending a track and field team. However, the problem of how to compensate for the loss of salary for football players due to participating in the World Games is difficult to solve for a while, and efforts are currently being made. Recently, a Dutch travel agency has purchased 1,000 World Games tickets to meet the needs of 1,000 spectators who will go to watch the Dutch football team's match on the day or the day before. From this, it can be seen that the Netherlands is enthusiastic about football, and of course no one will undermine the legitimate hope of participating this time.

News from the Shanghai West People's Livelihood Education Experiment Area, Jointly Sponsored by the Education Bureau and Daxia University

The Shanghai West People's Livelihood Education Experiment Area, jointly sponsored by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, Daxia University, and the Nian Er (February 2nd) Movement Promotion Association, has been conducting experimental work since August of last year. Today marks the first anniversary, and a week-long commemorative meeting will be held at the general counseling center in the area. Details are as follows:

Commemorative Program

(1) Commemorative Ceremony (8:00 AM to 10:00 AM); (2) Friends' Gathering (10:00 AM to 11:00 AM) (Carriage performance, playing the qin, chess, abacus practice, exercises, etc.); (3) Medical Treatment by Friends (Mobile medical team, 1:30 PM to 2:00 PM); (4) Crossword Competition (2:00 PM to 3:00 PM); (5) Weaving Competition (3:00 PM to 4:00 PM); (6) Exhibition of Friends' Achievements; (7) Exhibition of Weaving Products; (8) Exhibition of Various Teaching Materials; (9) Exhibition of Various Regulations; (10) Exhibition of Books from This Area; (11) Entertainment (Activity education film of this area, 7:00 PM at Daxia University).

Experimental Area

The area is located near Daxia University in western Shanghai and is jointly sponsored by the Municipal Education Bureau, Daxia University, and the Nian Er Movement Promotion Association. The total area is 40 square li, with more than 2,000 households and a population of more than 12,000. Of the residents in the area, 80% are farmers, 10% are workers, and 5% are rickshaw pullers. Many are also engaged in small businesses. The livelihood of the residents in the area, except for a few who are engaged in business and own assets, is generally not very prosperous. More than 80% of adults are illiterate. Therefore, the area aims to experiment with livelihood-based education, promote the use of local products, practice social thrift, strive for social production, develop the rural economy, improve the lives of the residents in the area, promote the various movements stipulated by the central government, and jointly seek the revitalization of the Chinese nation.

Educational Situation

Teaching methods: (A) Mobile teaching: (1) Meetings, commemorative gatherings, entertainment performances, flag-raising ceremonies, problem discussions, etc.; (2) Collective practice: current affairs reports, common sense guidance, homework study, Nian Er lectures, etc.; (3) Visits: medical visits, work visits, friendship visits, life visits, etc.; (4) Exhibitions: agricultural exhibitions, local product exhibitions, book exhibitions, health exhibitions, etc.; (B) Teaching according to the time: (1) Sunny days: outdoor teaching; (2) Rainy days: indoor teaching; (3) Hot weather: teaching in cool places; (4) Cold weather: teaching around a stove. Teaching tools include popular education and various education boxes, bringing education to the door.

Business Overview

In addition to the 205 yuan allocated monthly from the 350 yuan subsidized by the Municipal Education Bureau to the Nian Er Movement Promotion Association, Daxia University provides an annual subsidy of 500 yuan. The following businesses have been carried out in the past year: West Nian Er Society, Jinjia Lane Nian Er Society, Xujia Zhai Nian Er Society, and the promotion of Nian Er Society, etc. Each society aims to reach 200 people this year. The main economic activity groups include rickshaw puller cooperative groups, laundry cooperative groups, weaving cooperative groups, and planting cooperative groups, etc. Cooperating in businesses such as joint production, sales, consumption, savings, security, fire protection, hygiene, entertainment, road construction, river dredging, afforestation, and disaster prevention, etc.

The Basic Work of Educational and Career Guidance (Part Two)

— He Qing

I. Investigating Students' Individual Situations As we mentioned earlier, students' individual situations vary. In superficial aspects, such as age, gender, and place of origin, there is no need to discuss them. In more important aspects, such as general intelligence, special abilities, academic performance, physical condition, extracurricular activities, aspirations, interests, and family environment, there are also differences. These differences have different effects on the problems that arise. In addition to these situations, individual problems are also included, because educational problems and career problems should be distinguished, and the content of educational problems or career problems can be further analyzed.

Investigating students' situations includes these items, and it cannot be completed in a short time. Especially in schools with a large number of students, it must be carried out at any time during the weekdays. It is best to do so within the last year, because if the time is too long, it will become ineffective and inaccurate when it is applied. This kind of investigation must adopt the prescribed forms and be carried out effectively. Some of the materials required can be provided by the students themselves, and some need to be collected from various sources.

Although materials can be collected from various sources, this kind of investigation must be centrally managed and directed by designated persons responsible for guidance and planning. All teachers and staff in the school should assist and cooperate in the investigation work, but if there is no one in charge, it will not be able to continue and achieve satisfactory results. With an investigation, there will be a solid basis when implementing guidance, and the proposed solutions will be effective. Therefore, this kind of investigation is one of the basic works in guidance.

II. Collecting School and Career Materials In order to solve any guidance problem, in addition to clearly understanding the individual's situation as a basis, the career materials related to the problem should also be collected completely. Educational problems must have a list of regulations of various advanced schools (universities) or other materials for reference. Career problems must have investigations on career content, needs, and opportunities. These two kinds of materials have basic importance, and they cannot be completed in a short time. They must be solicited at any time during the weekdays in order to be sufficient. The reference materials on schools are naturally limited to those that have a considerable relationship with the students of this school. As for the career references, they should be limited to the scope related to the students of this school and the local community. Neither is broad and universal, so it may not be the same for schools in different regions. As for collection and investigation, some materials need to be carried out independently by each school, some can be done in cooperation with several schools, and some have already had considerable investigations by other agencies, which can be conveniently adopted. How to proceed should be decided according to the situation. In any case, in a school that implements guidance, there must be a person in charge of planning, organizing, and preserving various investigation materials. This work is as important as the management of investigating individual situations. It can also be done by one person, because both sides of the investigation work, as well as other guidance work, require a long time and energy, so it is best to have a full-time career guidance officer to avoid being added incidentally to other teachers and staff, so that they cannot have sufficient care.

III. Implementing Individual Guidance After investigating the students' situations, it is not enough to just save the results of the investigation. The purpose of the investigation is to serve as a basis for guidance, so guidance is a method and a step in the process, not the ultimate goal. When investigating, individual problems have been discovered, and then practical guidance should be implemented according to the individual problems and referring to all relevant materials. Whether it is an educational problem or a career problem, it must be realistic individual guidance in order to hope to get a solution. The so-called individual guidance is that the person in charge of guidance holds individual talks with students, discusses the students' problems, provides relevant references, and suggests solutions. This kind of individual talk is best concentrated and undertaken by the commissioner responsible for guidance, but sometimes the assistance of other teachers and staff is also needed. This kind of talk is not limited to one time. The number of times depends on the nature of the problem, and it cannot be fixed at one time for each person, or a few minutes each time. It must be flexible according to the individual situation.

Although individual guidance should be the responsibility of a special person, the guidance given often needs to be based on references from all parties. The plan for further study or further education should sometimes consult the teachers concerned. The economic situation and family environment should be requested from the parents. The health situation should refer to the doctor's opinion. Other aspects related to the problem should also be sought for suggestions. Therefore, the person in charge of guidance should become the center of guidance, integrating the opinions of all parties, and implementing the methods of disposal. It is not a hasty, arbitrary, or simple task, nor can it be completed temporarily or at the last minute.

IV. Contacting All Parties Outside the School Whether it is an educational problem or a career problem, students will have relationships with all parties outside the school, and career problems are even more so. Students going on to further education will have relationships with higher-level schools. If the school in charge of guidance can have considerable contact with each school, or invite the person in charge of each school to give a lecture at the school, or arrange for students of this school to visit each school, or have other contacts, it can provide many conveniences for students. As for students seeking employment, they need career opportunities. This kind of opportunity must be generated by students having considerable contact with various organizations in society.

An important purpose of contact is to express the achievements of this school. For schools going on to further education and for organizations seeking employment, a school must be able to express where it can contribute in order to arouse the possibility of cooperation. This kind of publicity should naturally be based on facts. If the school's performance is poor, society will naturally not be willing to cooperate, and students will feel that their way out is difficult. Therefore, contact with all parties is not an empty exchange or a false courtesy, but a pursuit of cooperation based on achievements.

The work of contact should also be the responsibility of a special person, and it cannot be arbitrarily entrusted to anyone. The person in charge of guidance can, of course, also take on this part of the work, but if it is too busy due to other work, or there are other inconvenient reasons, another person can be responsible. It is most appropriate for the leader of the school to take on the task because of the convenience of the position. No matter who takes on the task, this work should always be regarded as a formal part of guidance.

The above four types of work, we believe, are the most basic work for secondary schools to implement educational or career guidance. If these items can be fully and effectively implemented, even without other work, guidance can have a good effect. From these types of work, we can see that guidance is a part of education, which should be implemented on weekdays and focus on individual guidance. If we can recognize these tasks, the incorrect concepts of guidance can also be eliminated.

However, these tasks have a common prerequisite, that is, no matter which part of the work, there should be a special person in charge. It can also be said that to carry out educational and career guidance, there must be a special person to plan and implement it, and then it can be properly implemented and have substantial results. Without a special person, this career has nothing to rely on, which is equivalent to a mere formality. Therefore, those who intend to implement educational or career guidance must recognize the importance and long-term nature of this work and entrust the responsible person to plan and implement it. Then we can hope for the development of this career and that students can get more real benefits. (End)
